  657. I have very fine “fly away “hair and most styling products end up leaving my hair either to “gummy” feeling or looking oily and flatten out the roots. I was amazed my hair didn’t “fall flat” in the humid condition nor did it feel tacky.<br /><br />I woke up the next morning, combed my hair, fluffed the roots with my fingertips, added a bit more of the powder to the crown and it looked great, no tacky residue, easy to comb through.<br /><br />I had no troubles combing my hair out once the powder was applied the first night or the last two mornings.<br />Last night I used a bit of salt water spray to “poof” it up, used a little bit of hair spray on the crown and was out the door for the evening. I got up this morning and was surprised to find it still had “fluff” left at the root.<br /><br />Washed my hair earlier and the powder residue was nonexistent, couldn’t even tell I had used anything in my hair two days in row. I parted my hair and sprinkled the power into the part section, did this with five different section from side to side and across crown, used very little powder, once I had the powder applied, I “finger&#34; fluffed/combed the roots, and was done.<br /><br />This stuff turned into a godsend for my thin hair!
